30/03/2020, 1:28 am - Nayanika: The stars make constellations on her back
Fireflies around her hair, jet black.

Clear Water through her veins, 
with the sparkle of a thousand diamonds.
Flowers grow at her fingertips, 
strength greater than the twelve titans.

Her womb seals her greatest love, 
I, she says, am an endowment from the heaven above.

She plucked out the honeyed fruits
To make my hunger disappear.
But my voracious soul, 
was never satiated with gifts so mere.

So I decided to slash her down,
burn her blind.
I Decided to satisfy 
My belly and my mind.

I didn’t fathom,
When the stars started to hide behind the haze
The fireflies started blowing chunks of blaze.
The water now matched with a colour of grey,
The flowers exhibited the first sign of decay.

What do I do O’mother? 
Now that it’s my time to give back what I took
Your sacrifices made me who I am,
But none of that I understood.

What do I do O’mother?
Now that my own life is in jeopardy 
Do I cry till my tears extinguish your fire;
Or do I get gulped down from where I came, like you desire?

05/04/2020, 8:31 pm - Nayanika: She’s beautiful. When she finally goes out at 7:45am for her classes, her dupatta sliding off from one shoulder, her earrings making music while she fastens her pace. “Don’t look at her” my mom interrupts, “She’s a witch, everyone knows that she does black magic”. I close the curtains and go back to the breakfast table. “It’s true” she continues, “the cat that entered her house that day searching for food, the neighbours found it dead near the lane, it’s eyes gouged out by a fork lying near it”. “And that poor boy”, my sister adds, “the guy she liked, he is nowhere to be found; god knows what she did to him”. I run upstairs to my room.  I hate how people keep judging her. She’s never the problem. I remember how she told me that her boyfriend was eating her brains out. Taking out the shiny silver one, from my favourite fork collection, I punctured through the fleshy brain while blood oozed out. “This boy never has his breakfast properly”, my mother complained from downstairs.

06/04/2020, 10:43 pm - Nayanika: In this unfortunate time of quarantine due to the danger of COVID-19 aka Corona Virus pandemic, *JIST CULTURAL WELFARE SOCIETY (JCWS)* wants to make the best out of this situation.

*JCWS* is organising an *online competition* of a few categories (as mentioned below).

We hereby request the interested students to participate in these events and have fun along the process while staying at home. Share your posts in *Facebook or Instagram (IGTV)* mentioning your *NAME, COLLEGE/SCHOOL/UNIVERSITY, DEPARTMENT, SEMESTER and EVENT CATEGORY of your submission* and *tag JCWS* on each platform. 

JCWS Facebook page :
https://m.facebook.com/JIST-Cultural-Welfare-Society-762612187279465/

JCWS Instagram handle :
https://instagram.com/jcws_inst?igshid=109o9lsyeorh6

We have respective judges from each event. Winners of each category will be awarded (after the end of this quarantine period) and will be shared on our Facebook page and Instagram account.

*LAST DATE OF SUBMISSION : 11:59 PM, 5th April, 2020*
